#GeneA_Pan] tested for an excess of RDGVS in samples with LOH compared to in samples without LOH in a pan-cancer. '1' : LOH sample, '0': noLOH sample.

#GeneA_OV_type2] tested for an excess of RDGVs in samples of OV versus samples of the other cancer types. '1' : OV-LOH sample, '0': nonOV-LOH sample. 'NA': noLOH sample.
#gene_GeneA:Germline] genotype column which contain '1' (with rare damaging germline variants) or '0' (without rare damaging germline variants).
